***aap.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aap.html>aap</a> (2105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">āpe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*apo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*apô</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***aar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aar.html>aar</a> (41162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">âer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ār</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ahaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aar.html>aar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aren.html>aren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aar.html>aartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>ear (of corn, grain etc.)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">āer</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardappel.html>aardappel</a> (10523)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">soil, earth, ground</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:appel.html>appel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">apple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> English <i>earthapple</i>; French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">pomme <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:terre.html>terre</a></i>, Luxembourgish <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb">Gromper</i> (originally "ground pear"), German regionally both <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Erdapfel</i> ("earth apple") and <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Grundbirne</i> ("ground pear")
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>potato</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardbei.html>aardbei</a> (17709)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">erdbere</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*erdberi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*erþōbazją</i>. Compare German <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">Erdbeere</i>, West Frisian <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">ierdbei</i>, Danish <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">jordbær</i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aardbei.html>aardbei</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aardbeien.html>aardbeien</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aardbeitje.html>aardbeitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aarden.html>aarden</a> (52522)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">erdijn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*irthīn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*irþīnaz</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>. Reformed by analogy with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarden.html>aarden</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>earthen, made of soil</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> etc., made of pottery made from soil</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarden.html>aarden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ground, connect an electrical conductor as a safety outlet</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to commit to the earth, bury
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begraven.html>begraven</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ter.html>ter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bestellen.html>bestellen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection_2">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aard.html>aard</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarden.html>aarden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (<i>used with <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> ...)</i> to take after, share (notably inherited) traits with (notably an ancestor)</li></ol>

***aardkloot.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardkloot.html>aardkloot</a> (77575)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aard.html>aard</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">earth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kloot.html>kloot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lump, clod</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aardkloot.html>aardkloot</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aardkloot.html>aardkloten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aardkloot.html>aardklootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated, poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Planet Earth
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oneerlijk.html>oneerlijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardkloot.html>aardkloot</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">How unfair life <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> on this planet of ours!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> any (<a href = vnd.unilang:rocky.html>rocky</a>) planet</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:kloot.html>Kloot</a></i>, when used on its own, <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> developed into a vulgar synonym for <i><a href = vnd.unilang:testikel.html>testikel</a></i>, meaning <i>testicle</i> and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used as an expletive corresponding with <i>bollocks</i>. In the compound noun <i><a href = vnd.unilang:aardkloot.html>aardkloot</a></i>, however, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:kloot.html>kloot</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> retained its original meaning of ‘lump of earth’ and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not usually considered offensive. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> restricted to literary or ironic <a href = vnd.unilang:registers.html>registers</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">planet earth</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aardbol.html>aardbol</a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:blauwe.html>blauwe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:planeet.html>planeet</a></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:aardkloot.html>aardkloot</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:verouderd.html>verouderd</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bolvormig.html>bolvormige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:planeet.html>planeet</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blauwe.html>blauwe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:planeet.html>planeet</a>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aartsvijand.html>aartsvijand</a> (24297)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarts-.html>aarts-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">arch-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vijand.html>vijand</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">enemy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">archfiend</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Erzfeind</i>.
</p>

***aarzelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aarzelen.html>aarzelen</a> (12871)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">erselen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">arselen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to step back, to retreat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, frequentative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ersen</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aers</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">buttocks</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aars.html>aars</a></i>). Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">arsle</i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarzelen.html>aarzelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hesitate</li></ol>

***aas.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aas.html>aas</a> (5116)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">âes</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ās</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ēsaz</i>.

</p>
<ol><li>bait</li>
<li>carrion</li></ol>

<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ase</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aes</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">as</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">as</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aaseter.html>aaseter</a> (110082)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aas.html>aas</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>eten</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aas.html>aas</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">carrion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gier.html>gier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vulture</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:abacus.html>abacus</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἄβαξ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ábax</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">arithmetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:abacus.html>abacus</a></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">arithmetic calculation device, usually with beads on rods</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.

<p>From American <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">abulón</i>, from an indigenous language of the Monterey Bay area such as Rumsen/<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Ohlone_language" class="extiw" title="w:Southern Ohlone language">Southern Ohlone</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="css">aūlun</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">red <a href = vnd.unilang:abalone.html>abalone</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Pinkabalone_300.jpg/220px-Pinkabalone_300.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="144" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Pinkabalone_300.jpg/330px-Pinkabalone_300.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Pinkabalone_300.jpg/440px-Pinkabalone_300.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1253" data-file-height="819" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>Pink <a href = vnd.unilang:abalone.html>abalone</a>.</div></div></div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:abalone.html>abalone</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">abalones</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Canada, US<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An edible univalve mollusc of the genus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:haliotis.html>Haliotis</a></i>, having a shell lined with mother-of-pearl. <span class="defdate">[from mid-19th century]</span><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup></li>

***abces.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:abces.html>abces</a> (55214)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">abscessus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a going away; gathering of humors, abscess</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">abscēdō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">go away, depart</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">abs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">away from</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cēdō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">go</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:abnormaal.html>abnormaal</a> (11277)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">abnormal</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">abnormal</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ab-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:normaal.html>normaal</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:abnormaal.html>abnormaal</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:abnormaal.html>abnormaler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">abnormaalst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>abnormal (not conforming to rule or system)</li></ol>

***abominabel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:abominabel.html>abominabel</a> (58272)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:abominabel.html>abominabel</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">abhominabel</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">abominable</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">abominabilis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:abominabel.html>abominabel</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:abominabel.html>abominabeler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">abominabelst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>abominable, hateful, terrible; detestable; loathsome</li></ol>
